<analysis>
The AI engineer's work focused on a comprehensive migration of the BuildConnect application from a legacy React framework to Next.js (App Router). The primary goal was to replicate the  design, ensuring full English and Icelandic localization. Key efforts involved replicating UI components, establishing correct routing for various category pages and a 3-step job posting wizard, and resolving environmental conflicts (React vs. Next.js on port 3000). The AI meticulously addressed hydration errors, API integration issues by correcting backend URLs and environment variable usage, and systematically eliminated all hardcoded Norwegian text in favor of the translation system. The latest achievement was implementing the -style  page, with the session concluding on a user's query about a Git/GitHub saving issue, which the AI correctly deferred to the support agent due to access constraints.
</analysis>

<product_requirements>
The BuildConnect application aims to be a construction services marketplace, replicating 's design and functionality with full English and Icelandic localization. The initial MVP required a redesigned homepage and a 3-step job posting wizard. Key features included precise UI/UX replication of the Header, Hero, navigation, and All Categories sections. A new company registration page was a core requirement. The foundational directive was a complete migration from React to Next.js, with all subsequent development solely within the Next.js application. Specific in-trajectory requests included applying 's color palette, maintaining the exact layout of the original React application (including  and ), ensuring the Start here button routes to , and creating specialized category pages (e.g., Automotive, Cleaning, Moving) or directing to a generic job posting wizard, all while ensuring all content is properly localized and removing all Norwegian text. The  page required a specific  grid-based layout.
</product_requirements>
